- FULL SCREEN: no tab bar, no header, no SOS button (already in SOS)

- Breathing exercise: primary highlighted action
- No analytics tracking on SOS screen (privacy)
- All actions free regardless of subscription

### WF-024: Diary List

**Flow:** UF-005 | **Story:** US-016 | **Priority:** P0

- Haptic: optional phase-change vibration
- Pause: freezes animation and timer
- Complete: shows WF-034

---

## 8. Mini-courses

### WF-036: Course Catalog

**Flow:** UF-007 | **Story:** US-024 | **Priority:** P1
